' 店铺
组件暂停重画 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄)
组件插入元素 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列表头, 0, 0, 1)
组件置选择框元素属性 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列表头, 0, 0, 0, 到整数 (&_商品销售报表_表头回调), 位或 (#布局模式_左边_居中, #布局模式_顶边_居中), , , 16, 16, 0, #复选框, , 16, 16, )
组件置选择框元素数据 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列表头, 0, 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, , 0, 1)
组件插入元素 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列项目, 0, 0, 0)
组件置选择框元素属性 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列项目, 0, 0, 0, 到整数 (&_商品销售报表_表头回调), 位或 (#布局模式_左边_居中, #布局模式_顶边_居中), , , 16, 16, 0, #复选框, , 16, 16, )
窗口_商品销售报表.店铺名称_超级列表框EX.删除项目 (-1, )
.如果 (等于 (全局_店铺权限操作, “”))
    执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL读取_报表, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (“SELECT '0' AS akufang, '总库' AS btitle”), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))
.否则
    执行SQL语句 (全_MySQL读取_报表, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (相加 (“SELECT id AS akufang,CASE WHEN id='0' THEN '总库' ELSE title END AS btitle FROM xipunum_erp_type WHERE type='商铺' AND superior='0' AND id in (”, 全局_店铺权限操作, “) UNION ALL SELECT '0' AS akufang, '总库' AS btitle FROM dual WHERE '0' IN (”, 全局_店铺权限操作, “) ORDER BY akufang='0' DESC, akufang”)), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))
.如果结束

赋值 (库房列表集句柄, 取记录集 (全_MySQL读取_报表))
.如果真 (不等于 (库房列表集句柄, 0))
    赋值 (库房数量, 取记录集行数 (库房列表集句柄))
    .如果真 (大于 (库房数量, 0))
        窗口_商品销售报表.店铺名称_超级列表框EX.插入项目 (-1, 库房数量, , 30)
        .计次循环首 (库房数量, 库房计次)
            赋值 (库房列表数据id, “”)
            赋值 (库房列表数据名称, “”)
            读字段值 (库房列表集句柄, “akufang”, 库房列表数据id)
            读字段值 (库房列表集句柄, “btitle”, 库房列表数据名称)
            .如果 (等于 (库房计次, 1))
                组件置选择框元素数据 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列项目, 相减 (库房计次, 1), 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, , 0, 1)
            .否则
                组件置选择框元素数据 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄, #元素归属_超列项目, 相减 (库房计次, 1), 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, , 0, 0)
            .如果结束
            窗口_商品销售报表.店铺名称_超级列表框EX.置项目文本 (相减 (库房计次, 1), 1, 取文本右边 (相加 (“000”, 到文本 (库房计次)), 取文本长度 (到文本 (库房数量))))
            窗口_商品销售报表.店铺名称_超级列表框EX.置项目文本 (相减 (库房计次, 1), 2, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (库房列表数据名称), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )))
            窗口_商品销售报表.店铺名称_超级列表框EX.置项目文本 (相减 (库房计次, 1), 3, 到文本 (编码转换 (到字节集 (库房列表数据id), #编码_UTF_8, #编码_GBK, )))
            到下一行 (库房列表集句柄)
        .计次循环尾 ()
    .如果真结束
    释放记录集 (库房列表集句柄)
.如果真结束
组件允许重画 (店铺名称_超级列表框组件句柄)
.如果真 (小于或等于 (库房数量, 1))
    赋值 (窗口_商品销售报表.店铺名称_超级列表框EX.禁止, 真)
.如果真结束

30, 3 )) AS tol_jinzhong,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.zongzhong),0), 3 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 3 )) AS tol_zhongliang,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.xiaoshoujia),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_yingshou,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.yingshou),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_shishou,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.xiaoshougf*tol.xsjinzhong),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_xsgongfei,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.xiaoshoufj),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_xsfujia,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.gongfeilr),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_gongfeilr FROM (SELECT COALESCE ( e1.id, e2.id, '0' ) AS guigeid,b.kufang AS kufangid,b.creationtime AS chukutime,f.settlement_number AS djdingdanbian,f.customer_code as djkhbianma,k.`name` as djkhname,k.tel as djkhtel,f.presale_number as djysdanhao,o.deposit as djdingjin,l.jin_zhong as hsjinzhong,l.settlement as hsjine,f.salesman as djyewu,f.settlement as sdjhishou,f.taxamount as djshuijin,CONCAT(a.cjuser, '(', j.name, ')') AS djccjuser,f.pling as djpiling,b.poduct_code as bianma,a.product_name as mingcheng,CASE WHEN b.kufang = '0' THEN '总库' ELSE h.title END AS kufang,g.title as gongchang,a.item_number as kuanhao,CASE WHEN COALESCE(d.title, '' ) = '' THEN '未匹配' ELSE d.title END AS pinlei,COALESCE (e1.title,e2.title, '未匹配' ) AS guige,a.caizhi as caizhi,a.single as danzhong,b.quantity as xsshuliang,b.net_weight as xsjinzhong,CAST(ROUND(CASE WHEN COALESCE(i.lingxiao, '') = '是' THEN b.net_weight ELSE a.weight / NULLIF(a.quantity, 0) * b.quantity END, 3 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30,3 )) AS zongzhong,b.gold_price as kejia,b.xiao_amount as xiaoshoujia,b.settlement as yingshou,c.basic_cost as chengbengf,c.company_surcharge as chengbenfj,c.cost_price as chengben,b.sales_cost as xiaoshougf,b.sales_surcharge as xiaoshoufj,b.zhekou as zhekou,a.quandu as quankou,c.company_condition as chengse,a.sales_unit as danwei,m.`name` as daogou,b.pling as xqpiling,CAST(ROUND((COALESCE ( b.sales_cost, 0 )-COALESCE ( c.basic_cost, 0 ))*COALESCE ( b.net_weight, 0 )+COALESCE ( b.sales_surcharge, 0 )-COALESCE ( c.company_surcharge, 0 ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS gongfeilr FROM xipunum_erp_outbound AS b INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_shop AS a ON a.poduct_code = b.poduct_code INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_outbound_order AS f ON f.id = b.order_id INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store AS c ON c.poduct_code = a.poduct_code INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store_order AS n ON n.id = c.order_id LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_type AS h ON h.id = b.kufang  INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_about AS g ON g.id = n.factory LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_ksiamges AS i ON i.kuanhao = a.item_number AND a.item_number != '' LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS e1 ON e1.id = i.specification_id AND a.item_number IS NOT NULL AND a.item_number != '' LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS e2 ON e2.id = a.specification_id AND a.specification_id IS NOT NULL AND a.specification_id != '' LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_category AS d ON d.id = COALESCE ( e1.category_id, e2.category_id ) AND COALESCE ( e1.category_id, e2.category_id ) IS NOT NULL  LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS j ON j.user = f.cjuser LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_member AS k ON k.customer_code = f.customer_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_retreat_order AS l ON l.retrea_umber = f.retrea_umber LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS m ON m.USER = b.shopping_guide  LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_presale_order AS o ON o.presale_umber = f.presale_number WHERE (a.poduct_code LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.fu_code LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.product_name LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.item_number LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.caizhi LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR g.title LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR g.jianxie LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR k.memberid LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR k.NAME LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR k.tel LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%'  OR f.xsfactory LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%') ”, 查找信息客户, “ and b.creationtime>='”, 查找开始日期, “' and b.creationtime<'”, 查找结束日期, “' ”, 查找信息库房, 查找信息批零, 查找信息金重, “ ORDER BY b.id desc) as tol ”, 查找信息规格, “ ORDER BY tol.chukutime DESC”)), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))

) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 3 )) AS tol_zhongliang,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.chengbengf*tol.xsjinzhong),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_cbgongfei,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.chengbenfj),0), 2 ) AS 2 )) AS tol_xsgongfei,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.xiaoshoufj),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_xsfujia,CAST(ROUND(COALESCE (sum(tol.xiaoshoujia),0), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS AS guige,a.caizhi as caizhi,a.single as danzhong,b.quantity as xsshuliang,b.net_weight as xsjinzhong,CAST(ROUND(CASE WHEN COALESCE(i.lingxiao, '') = '是' THEN b.net_weight ELSE a.weight / COALESCE ( tol.youhui, 0 ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS tol_youhui FROM (SELECT COALESCE ( e1.id, e2.id, '0' ) AS guigeid,b.kufang AS kufangid,b.creationtime AS chukutime,f.settlement_number AS djdingdanbian,f.customer_code as djkhbianma,k.`name` as djkhname,k.tel as djkhtel,f.presale_number as djysdanhao,o.deposit as djdingjin,l.jin_zhong as hsjinzhong,l.settlement as hsjine,f.salesman as djyewu,f.settlement as sdjhishou,f.taxamount as djshuijin,CONCAT(a.cjuser, '(', j.name, ')') AS djccjuser,f.pling as djpiling,b.poduct_code as bianma,a.product_name as mingcheng,CASE WHEN b.kufang = '0' THEN '总库' ELSE h.title END AS kufang,g.title as gongchang,a.item_number as kuanhao,CASE WHEN COALESCE(d.title, '' ) = '' THEN '未匹配' ELSE d.title END AS pinlei,COALESCE (e1.title,e2.title, '未匹配' ) AS guige,a.caizhi as caizhi,a.single as danzhong,b.quantity as xsshuliang,b.net_weight as xsjinzhong,CAST(ROUND(CASE WHEN COALESCE(i.lingxiao, '') = '是' THEN b.net_weight ELSE a.weight / NULLIF(a.quantity, 0) * b.quantity END, 3 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30,3 )) AS zongzhong,b.gold_price as kejia,b.xiao_amount as xiaoshoujia,b.settlement as yingshou,c.basic_cost as chengbengf,c.company_surcharge as chengbenfj,c.cost_price as chengben,b.sales_cost as xiaoshougf,b.sales_surcharge as xiaoshoufj,b.zhekou as zhekou,a.quandu as quankou,c.company_condition as chengse,a.sales_unit as danwei,m.`name` as daogou,b.pling as xqpiling,CAST(ROUND((COALESCE ( b.sales_cost, 0 )-COALESCE ( c.basic_cost, 0 ))*COALESCE ( b.net_weight, 0 )+COALESCE ( b.sales_surcharge, 0 )-COALESCE ( c.company_surcharge, 0 ), 2 ) AS DECIMAL ( 30, 2 )) AS gongfeilr,CASE WHEN f.sales_return = 1 THEN -f.youhui ELSE f.youhui END AS youhui FROM xipunum_erp_outbound AS b INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_shop AS a ON a.poduct_code = b.poduct_code INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_outbound_order AS f ON f.id = b.order_id INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store AS c ON c.poduct_code = a.poduct_code INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_store_order AS n ON n.id = c.order_id LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_type AS h ON h.id = b.kufang  INNER JOIN xipunum_erp_about AS g ON g.id = n.factory LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_ksiamges AS i ON i.kuanhao = a.item_number AND a.item_number != '' LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS e1 ON e1.id = i.specification_id AND a.item_number IS NOT NULL AND a.item_number != '' LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_specs AS e2 ON e2.id = a.specification_id AND a.specification_id IS NOT NULL AND a.specification_id != '' LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_category AS d ON d.id = COALESCE ( e1.category_id, e2.category_id ) AND COALESCE ( e1.category_id, e2.category_id ) IS NOT NULL  LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS j ON j.user = f.cjuser LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_member AS k ON k.customer_code = f.customer_code LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_retreat_order AS l ON l.retrea_umber = f.retrea_umber LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_user AS m ON m.USER = b.shopping_guide  LEFT JOIN xipunum_erp_presale_order AS o ON o.presale_umber = f.presale_number WHERE (a.poduct_code LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.fu_code LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.product_name LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.item_number LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR a.caizhi LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR g.title LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR g.jianxie LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR k.memberid LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR k.NAME LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR k.tel LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%' OR f.xsfactory LIKE '%”, 查找信息名称, “%') ”, 查找信息客户, “ and b.creationtime>='”, 按类型开始日期, “' and b.creationtime<'”, 按类型结束日期, “' ”, 查找信息库房, 查找信息批零, 查找信息金重, “ ORDER BY b.id desc) as tol ”, 查找信息规格, “ GROUP BY tol.djdingdanbian,tol.kufangid ORDER BY tol.chukutime DESC) as ddtol”)), #编码_GBK, #编码_UTF_8, )))
